[6] thinking: **Filtering monitor options**

I need to screen for monitors between 33 to 49 inches, focusing on specific checkboxes and price ranges, like 1000-2000. I think including 31.5-33.9 might cause issues, especially with potential overlaps, so it makes sense to manually exclude 32 inches. I need a QLED panel with 240Hz, so I'll search using "QLED 240Hz monitor" and apply the necessary filters. I might need to check details to avoid confusion between QLED and OLED, particularly for the Samsung Odyssey G9.

**Using filters for monitor search**

I might need to use a website like BestBuy and apply search filters for QLED monitors. I’ll set the screen size to 34-39.9 inches and 40+ inches, with a refresh rate of 240Hz, and specify the price range. I think selecting multiple values in one go could help, but I should be mindful of how clicking checkboxes might trigger page reloads and potentially lead to stale references. 

Using locators by label names, like `page.getByRole('checkbox', {name:'QLED'})`, seems safer since it avoids issues with reference IDs.

await page.getByPlaceholder('Min Price').fill('1000');
await page.getByPlaceholder('Max Price').fill('2000');
await page.getByRole('button', {name: 'Set'}).click();
